News Item Added Started at 31/12/2013 07:54:03
User ID      : 277
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25621
Title        : Myer offers free postage after website crash
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) goes into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers after its website crashed on Boxing Day. 
Script       : <div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. &nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	CEO Bernie Brookes has joined the company&rsquo;s social media voice in apologising for the technical glitch which crashed the site on Australia&rsquo;s biggest shopping day of the year. &nbsp;&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	While Myer claims only 1 per cent of its annual $2.8 billion in sales are generated online Mr Brookes has conceded the latest outage is a blow to the company&rsquo;s reputation as it strives to expand its online offering.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Mr Brookes has told media Myer&rsquo;s technical team are working with IBM in the US to identify the root cause of the problem which is understood to have been caused by a bug in the system causing the server to crash.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Myer Holdings reported a net profit of almost $130 million in the 2013 financial year.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Myer Holdings, ASX:MYR, Bernie Brookes
Stock Ticker : ASX:MYR

News Item Added Started at 31/12/2013 07:55:47
User ID      : 277
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25622
Title        : Forge chief shrugs off takeover speculation
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Forge Group Limited’s (ASX:FGE) chief shrugs off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike.  
Script       : <div>
	<span style="font-size: 12px;">Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. &nbsp;</span><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	Forge yesterday responded to its second price query from the Australian Securities Exchange in under a week.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	After surging more than 50 per cent yesterday the company highlighted its $830 million contract award to work on Gina Rinehart&#39;s Roy Hill iron ore project in Western Australia.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	After surging more than 40 per cent last week the company could only attribute the prior week&rsquo;s $40 million worth of contract awards for the rise. &nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The gains come after Forge dramatically plunged 90 per cent on the back of a profit warning issued in November.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	Forge Group reported a net profit of $62.9 million in the 2013 financial year.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Forge Group, Roy Hill, ASX:FGE, Gina Rinehart
Stock Ticker : ASX:FGE
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

News Item Added Started at 31/12/2013 09:19:33
User ID      : 277
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25623
Title        : Outlook: Aus shares set to slip into NYE
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Aus shares set to slip into NYE. A look at how 2012's best performer Maverick Drilling and Exploration Limited (ASX:MAD) and worst performer Aveo Group (ASX:AOG) fared in 2013.  
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market looks set to pause from the year&rsquo;s really and slip in the last day of the year. While Wall Street mainly finished weaker overnight the three major indexes have jumped more than 25 per cent this year.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Most global markets are also on track to book a bumper year of gains including the local benchmark which has advanced about 15 per cent over 2013. &nbsp; &nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Today&rsquo;s trading volumes are expected to be subdued over a shortened session - ahead of New Years celebrations and tomorrows public holiday before trade resumes again on Thursday.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>US economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The National Association of Realtors has shown pending American home sales firmed last month from the month before but remain lower over the year. The Pending Home Sales Index is based on signed contracts and gained 0.2 per cent to 101.7 in November but was 1.6 per cent lower from the year before.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Wall Street &lsquo;s major indexes started the week is soft yet mixed fashion: The Dow Jones Industrial Average booked its 51st record close this year, gaining 26 points to close at 16,504. The S&amp;P 500 dipped 0.33 points to close at 1,841. The NASDAQ eased 2 points to close at 4,154.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	European markets started the week in the red with UK stocks snapping six days of gains: London&rsquo;s FTSE lost 20 points, Paris lost 2 points and Frankfurt lost 37 points.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Across Asian the markets were mixed: Tokyo&rsquo;s Nikkei added 112 points, Hong Kong&rsquo;s Hang Seng added 2 points, and China&rsquo;s Shanghai Composite lost 4 points.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian share market climbed 0.6 per cent yesterday, extending a gain of 15 per cent gain over 2013: The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index rose 33 points to close at 5,357. On the futures market the SPI is 3 points lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Currencies&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is on track for its largest annual decline since 2008 against the greenback. At 8:30AM the Aussie has firmed from Monday&rsquo;s close and is buying $US0.8907, 54 Pence Sterling, 93.58 Yen and 64.58 Euro cents.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>2012 best and worst performers&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Last year&rsquo;s best performing stock Maverick Drilling and Exploration Limited (ASX:MAD) hasn&rsquo;t been so fortunate this year. The oil and gas explorer and producer&rsquo;s stock surged 227 per cent in 2012 but has fallen almost 40 per cent in 2013 on the back of disappointing drilling results. Michael Yeager was appointed CEO and Executive Chairman in October and said at the time the company is expected to grow significantly. Shares in Maverick Drilling and Exploration rose 1.15 per cent yesterday to end the session at $0.44.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Last year&rsquo;s work performing stock Aveo Group (ASX:AOG), formally FKP Property Group (ASX:FKP), has experienced a stellar turnaround over the past twelve months. Last year when the property and investment company was trading under the name FKP Property Group its stock plunged 57 per cent over the 2012 calendar year. This year the company decided to refine its strategy and change its name to Aveo and has seen a share price jump of more than 88 per cent over the 2013 calendar year. Shares in Aveo Group jumped 7.04 per cent yesterday to end the session at $2.13.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Ex-dividends next week</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Clime Capital (ASX:CAM) paying a 1 cent fully franked dividend&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Programmed Maintenance Services Limited (ASX:PRG) paying a 6 cent fully franked dividend&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	After a upbeat start to the week the price of gold has retreated $10.20 to $US1,204 an ounce for the February contract on Comex.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Silver has eased $0.43 to $19.62 for March.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Copper is flat at $3.38 a pound.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Oil has fallen $1.03 at $US99.29 a barrel for January light crude in New York.</div>

Keyword      : SPI 200, Gold, Silver, Copper, Oil, Currency, Maverick Drilling, Aveo Group, ASX:MAD, ASX:AOG, ASX:FKP, FKP Property Group
Stock Ticker : ASX:MAD, ASX:AOG, ASX:FKP
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

	Last year&rsquo;s work performing stock Aveo Group (ASX:AOG), formally FKP Property Group (ASX:FKP), has experienced a stellar turnaround over the past twelve months. Last year when the property and investment company was trading under the name FKP Property Group its stock plunged 57 per cent over the 2012 calendar year. This year the company decided to refine its strategy and change its name to Aveo and has seen a share price jump of more than 88 per cent over the 2013 calendar year. Shares in Aveo Group jumped 7.04 per cent yesterday to end the session at $2.13.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Ex-dividends next week</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Clime Capital (ASX:CAM) paying a 1 cent fully franked dividend&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Programmed Maintenance Services Limited (ASX:PRG) paying a 6 cent fully franked dividend&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	After a upbeat start to the week the price of gold has retreated $10.20 to $US1,204 an ounce for the February contract on Comex.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Silver has eased $0.43 to $19.62 for March.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Copper is flat at $3.38 a pound.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Oil has fallen $1.03 at $US99.29 a barrel for January light crude in New York.</div>

Title        : Outlook: Aus shares set to slip into NYE
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Aus shares set to slip into NYE. A look at how 2012's best performer Maverick Drilling and Exploration Limited (ASX:MAD) and worst performer Aveo Group (ASX:AOG) fared in 2013.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market looks set to pause from the year&rsquo;s really and slip in the last day of the year. While Wall Street mainly finished weaker overnight the three major indexes have jumped more than 25 per cent this year.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Most global markets are also on track to book a bumper year of gains including the local benchmark which has advanced about 15 per cent over 2013. &nbsp; &nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Today&rsquo;s trading volumes are expected to be subdued over a shortened session - ahead of New Years celebrations and tomorrows public holiday before trade resumes again on Thursday.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>US economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The National Association of Realtors has shown pending American home sales firmed last month from the month before but remain lower over the year. The Pending Home Sales Index is based on signed contracts and gained 0.2 per cent to 101.7 in November but was 1.6 per cent lower from the year before.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Wall Street &lsquo;s major indexes started the week is soft yet mixed fashion: The Dow Jones Industrial Average booked its 51st record close this year, gaining 26 points to close at 16,504. The S&amp;P 500 dipped 0.33 points to close at 1,841. The NASDAQ eased 2 points to close at 4,154.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	European markets started the week in the red with UK stocks snapping six days of gains: London&rsquo;s FTSE lost 20 points, Paris lost 2 points and Frankfurt lost 37 points.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Across Asian the markets were mixed: Tokyo&rsquo;s Nikkei added 112 points, Hong Kong&rsquo;s Hang Seng added 2 points, and China&rsquo;s Shanghai Composite lost 4 points.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian share market climbed 0.6 per cent yesterday, extending a gain of 15 per cent gain over 2013: The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index rose 33 points to close at 5,357. On the futures market the SPI is 3 points lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Currencies&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is on track for its largest annual decline since 2008 against the greenback. At 8:30AM the Aussie has firmed from Monday&rsquo;s close and is buying $US0.8907, 54 Pence Sterling, 93.58 Yen and 64.58 Euro cents.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>2012 best and worst performers&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Last year&rsquo;s best performing stock Maverick Drilling and Exploration Limited (ASX:MAD) hasn&rsquo;t been so fortunate this year. The oil and gas explorer and producer&rsquo;s stock surged 227 per cent in 2012 but has fallen almost 40 per cent in 2013 on the back of disappointing drilling results. Michael Yeager was appointed CEO and Executive Chairman in October and said at the time the company is expected to grow significantly. Shares in Maverick Drilling and Exploration rose 1.15 per cent yesterday to end the session at $0.44.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Last year&rsquo;s work performing stock Aveo Group (ASX:AOG), formally FKP Property Group (ASX:FKP), has experienced a stellar turnaround over the past twelve months. Last year when the property and investment company was trading under the name FKP Property Group its stock plunged 57 per cent over the 2012 calendar year. This year the company decided to refine its strategy and change its name to Aveo and has seen a share price jump of more than 88 per cent over the 2013 calendar year. Shares in Aveo Group jumped 7.04 per cent yesterday to end the session at $2.13.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Ex-dividends next week</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Clime Capital (ASX:CAM) paying a 1 cent fully franked dividend&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Programmed Maintenance Services Limited (ASX:PRG) paying a 6 cent fully franked dividend&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>

<div>
	Silver has eased $0.43 to $19.62 for March.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Copper is flat at $3.38 a pound.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Oil has fallen $1.03 at $US99.29 a barrel for January light crude in New York.</div>

Title        : Outlook: Aus shares set to slip into NYE
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Aus shares set to slip into NYE. A look at how 2012's best performer Maverick Drilling and Exploration Limited (ASX:MAD) and worst performer Aveo Group (ASX:AOG) fared in 2013.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market looks set to pause from the year&rsquo;s really and slip in the last day of the year. While Wall Street mainly finished weaker overnight the three major indexes have jumped more than 25 per cent this year.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Most global markets are also on track to book a bumper year of gains including the local benchmark which has advanced about 15 per cent over 2013. &nbsp; &nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Today&rsquo;s trading volumes are expected to be subdued over a shortened session - ahead of New Years celebrations tonight and tomorrow&#39;s public holiday before trade resumes again on Thursday.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>US economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The National Association of Realtors has shown pending American home sales firmed last month from the month before but remain lower over the year. The Pending Home Sales Index is based on signed contracts and gained 0.2 per cent to 101.7 in November but was 1.6 per cent lower from the year before.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Wall Street&#39;s major indexes started the week is soft yet mixed fashion: The Dow Jones Industrial Average booked its 51st record close this year, gaining 26 points to close at 16,504. The S&amp;P 500 dipped 0.33 points to close at 1,841. The NASDAQ eased 2 points to close at 4,154.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	European markets started the week in the red with UK stocks snapping six days of gains: London&rsquo;s FTSE lost 20 points, Paris lost 2 points and Frankfurt lost 37 points.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Across Asian the markets were mixed: Tokyo&rsquo;s Nikkei added 112 points, Hong Kong&rsquo;s Hang Seng added 2 points, and China&rsquo;s Shanghai Composite lost 4 points.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian share market climbed 0.6 per cent yesterday, extending a gain of 15 per cent gain over 2013: The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index rose 33 points to close at 5,357. On the futures market the SPI is 3 points lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Currencies&nbsp;</strong></div>

	&nbsp;</div>

<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>2012 best and worst performers&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Last year&rsquo;s best performing stock Maverick Drilling and Exploration Limited (ASX:MAD) has not been so fortunate this year. The oil and gas explorer and producer&rsquo;s stock surged 227 per cent in 2012 but has fallen almost 40 per cent in 2013 on the back of disappointing drilling results. Michael Yeager was appointed CEO and Executive Chairman in October and said at the time the company is expected to grow significantly. Shares in Maverick Drilling and Exploration rose 1.15 per cent yesterday to end the session at $0.44.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Last year&rsquo;s work performing stock Aveo Group (ASX:AOG), formally FKP Property Group (ASX:FKP), has experienced a stellar turnaround over the past twelve months. Last year when the property and investment company was trading under the name FKP Property Group its stock plunged 57 per cent over the 2012 calendar year. This year the company decided to refine its strategy and change its name to Aveo and has seen a share price jump of more than 88 per cent over the 2013 calendar year. Shares in Aveo Group jumped 7.04 per cent yesterday to end the session at $2.13.&nbsp;</div>

News ID      : 25624
Title        : Fortescue safety record questions raised
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Questions are raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited’s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner’s operations report the third fatality in three years. 

Script       : <div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the company&rsquo;s operations reported the third fatality in three years.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Special directions have now been issued from The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum to the Pilbara focussed iron ore miner geared at improving its safety procedures.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Regulatory intervention comes after Fortescue yesterday informed the market a contractor employee had died from an accident.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The 23-year old male is understood to have been working in the heavy vehicle workshop at the Christmas Creek site in Western Australia when the accident occurred.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Fortescue voluntarily initiated a temporary suspension of surface mining operations following the incident and told the market it expected regulatory investigations to start immediately. &nbsp;<br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Fortescue Metals Group reported a net profit of $1.9 billion in the 2013 financial year.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Fortescue Metals, ASX:FMG, Christmas Creek 
Stock Ticker : ASX:FMG

Title        : Newcrest Mining hopes for brighter 2014
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - With the price of gold on track to post its biggest annual slump in 30 years Newcrest Mining Limited (ASX:NCM) will be hoping for a brighter New Year. 
Script       : <div>
	<span style="font-size: 12px;">With the price of gold on track to post its biggest annual slump in 30 years Newcrest Mining Limited (ASX:NCM) will be hoping for a brighter New Year.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Australia&rsquo;s largest gold mining company has been battered this year with its stock sinking more than 60 per cent to $7.95 at yesterday&rsquo;s close.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The falls came over the same period the price of gold fell from about $US1,600 per ounce at the beginning of the year to about $US1,200 per ounce.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	After making a massive write-down mid-year the company attracted the attention of the corporate watchdog.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">In the past weeks Newcrest has warned it may face class action from shareholders who allege the company breached its continuous disclosure obligations.</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	However, a changing of the guard is near with long standing Chairman Don Mercer retiring and CEO Greg Robinson stepping down this month.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The new year will see new leadership with Peter Hay moving into the Chairman&rsquo;s role and former Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO) executive Sandeep Biswas appointed CEO.&nbsp;<br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Newcrest Mining reported a net loss of $5.7 billion in the 2013 financial year.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Newcrest Mining, ASX:NCM, ASX:RIO
Stock Ticker : ASX:NCM, ASX:RIO

Title        : Newcrest Mining hopes for brighter 2014
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - With the price of gold on track to post its biggest annual slump in 30 years Newcrest Mining Limited (ASX:NCM) will be hoping for a brighter New Year. 
Script       : <div>
	<span style="font-size: 12px;">With the price of gold on track to post its biggest annual slump in 30 years Newcrest Mining Limited (ASX:NCM) will be hoping for a brighter New Year.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Australia&rsquo;s largest gold mining company has been battered this year with its stock sinking more than 60 per cent to $7.95 at yesterday&rsquo;s close.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The falls came over the same period the price of gold fell from about $US1,600 per ounce at the beginning of the year to about $US1,200 per ounce.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	After making a massive write-down mid-year the company attracted the attention of the corporate watchdog.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">In the past weeks Newcrest has warned it may face class action from shareholders who allege the company breached its continuous disclosure obligations.</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	However, a changing of the guard is near with long standing Chairman Don Mercer retiring and CEO Greg Robinson stepping down this month.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The new year will see new leadership with Peter Hay moving into the Chairman&rsquo;s role and former Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO) executive Sandeep Biswas appointed CEO.&nbsp;<br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Newcrest Mining reported a net loss of $5.7 billion in the 2013 financial year.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Newcrest Mining, ASX:NCM, ASX:RIO
Stock Ticker : ASX:NCM, ASX:RIO

News ID      : 25624
Title        : Fortescue safety record questions raised
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Questions are raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited’s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner’s operations report the third fatality in three years.
Script       : <div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the company&rsquo;s operations reported the third fatality in three years.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Special directions have now been issued from The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum to the Pilbara focussed iron ore miner geared at improving its safety procedures.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Regulatory intervention comes after Fortescue yesterday informed the market a contractor employee had died from an accident.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The 23-year old male is understood to have been working in the heavy vehicle workshop at the Christmas Creek site in Western Australia when the accident occurred.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Fortescue voluntarily initiated a temporary suspension of surface mining operations following the incident and told the market it expected regulatory investigations to start immediately. &nbsp;<br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Fortescue Metals Group reported a net profit of $1.9 billion in the 2013 financial year.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Fortescue Metals, ASX:FMG, Christmas Creek 
Stock Ticker : ASX:FMG

News ID      : 25626
Title        : Neon Energy plunges after drilling update
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunge  after the oil and gas explorer updates the market on drilling developments offshore Vietnam. 

Script       : <div>
	<span style="font-size: 12px;">Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) have plunged in morning trade after the oil and gas explorer updated the market on drilling developments offshore Vietnam.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Drilling and evaluation at the Ca Ngu-1 exploration well, located in Block 120, have not shown commercial potential and as a result the location will be abandoned as an oil and gas discovery well.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	However, the company believes the presence of a combined gas and oil column in the Miocene highlights potential for significant discoveries elsewhere in Block 120.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Managing Director Ken Charsinsky says Ca Ngu-1 provided valuable new information which will influence the forward exploration program within the block.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Mr Charsinsky says the company is now eagerly anticipating the results of production testing of the Cua Lo-1 gas discovery well.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy had fallen more than 24 per cent in morning trade to $0.29.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Neon Energy booked a net loss of $2.6 million in the first half of the 2013 calendar year.</div>
Keyword      : Neon Energy, ASX:NEN, Ca Ngu-1, 
Stock Ticker : ASX:NEN

News ID      : 25627
Title        : Macquarie Group leads IPO boom in 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - As the IPO market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. 
Script       : <div>
	<span style="font-size: 12px;">As the IPO market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 percent market share in equity capital market transactions followed by UBS with a 27 per cent share, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Macquarie scored roles on some of the year&rsquo;s largest initial public offerings including Pact Group Holdings Limited (ASX:PGH) and Nine Entertainment Co Holdings Limited (ASX:NEC).</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Co-head of equity capital markets Hugh Falcon told Bloomberg Macquarie had a great window where both vendors and investors were getting a win-win.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Macquarie have gained about 50 per cent in 2013, compared to a benchmark S&amp;P/ASX 200 rise of about 15 per cent over the year.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Macquarie Group reported a net profit of $503 million in the six months to the end of September 2013.&nbsp;</div>

Keyword      : Macquarie Group, ASX:MQGDA, ASX:MQG, ASX:PGH, ASX:NEC
Stock Ticker : ASX:MQG, ASX:PGH, ASX:NEC

News Item Update Started at 31/12/2013 15:20:32
User ID      : 277
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25628
Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red. 
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

News Item Update Started at 31/12/2013 15:20:32
User ID      : 277
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25628
Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red. 
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>

Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

Keyword      : S&P/ASX 200, Crude Oil, Gold, BHP Billiton, ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG
Stock Ticker : ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG

	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

Keyword      : S&P/ASX 200, Crude Oil, Gold, BHP Billiton, ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG

News Item Update Started at 31/12/2013 15:26:38
User ID      : 292
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25628
Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>

	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>

	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>

<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>

<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>

News Item Update Started at 31/12/2013 15:26:38
User ID      : 292
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25628
Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

Keyword      : S&P/ASX 200, Crude Oil, Gold, BHP Billiton, ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG
Stock Ticker : ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG

Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

Keyword      : S&P/ASX 200, Crude Oil, Gold, BHP Billiton, ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG
Stock Ticker : ASX:BHP, ASX:FMG, ASX:MYR, ASX:NEN, ASX:MQG

News Item Update Started at 31/12/2013 15:26:39
User ID      : 292
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25628
Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>

	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

News Item Update Started at 31/12/2013 15:26:39
User ID      : 292
Host Address : 150.101.192.132
News ID      : 25628
Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Reserve Bank of Australia (RBA) has shown demand for credit from Australian households and businesses remained subdued last month. The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Company news</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP) is just one of Western Australia&rsquo;s major miners who will keeping a close eye on Tropical Cyclone Christine as it crosses the coast. Most of Australia&rsquo;s iron ore exports came to a standstill over the weekend with authorities having since issued a Red Alert for Karratha and Port Hedland last night. Shares in BHP Billiton ended 2013 0.08 per cent lower at $37.99.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	With its website still offline after it crashed on Boxing Day Myer Holdings Limited (ASX:MYR) has gone into repair mode to compensate frustrated customers. The department store retailer will offer internet shoppers free postage and more online discounts when its website gets back into action. Shares in Myer Holdings ended 2013 0.72 per cent lower at $2.75.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Questions have been raised over Fortescue Metals Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FMG) safety record after the miner yesterday reported the third fatality at its operations in three years. The West Australian Department of Mines and Petroleum has now issued special directions geared to improving Fortescue&rsquo;s safety procedures.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	As the Initial Public Offering (IPO) market heated up this year Macquarie Group (ASX:MQGDA) took the lead for Australian equity underwriters for the first time since 2004. The nation&rsquo;s largest investment bank took a 29 per cent market share in equity capital market transactions, according to Bloomberg data.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Forge Group Limited&rsquo;s (ASX:FGE) chief has shrugged off speculation the engineering company is a takeover target following its significant share price spike over the past week. CEO David Simpson reportedly denied the rumours when asked by media and instead pointed to the company&rsquo;s latest contract awards as reason for the gains.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	Shares in Neon Energy Limited (ASX:NEN) plunged almost 30 per cent after the oil and gas explorer updated told the market one of its exploration wells offshore Vietnam has not shown commercial potential.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Best and worst performers</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The best performing sector was industrials, adding 4 points to close at 3,969.</div>
<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>

Title        : Market Wrap: ASX posts 15% gain over 2013
Description  : 31 Dec 2013 - ASX posts 15% gain over 2013. The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year, but ended the last session of the year in the red.
Script       : <div>
	The Australian share market has posted a 15 per cent gain over the year but ended the last day of the year in the red.&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12px;">Local stocks slipped early and hovered near the opening mark through a subdued session of trade.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Most sectors finished lower, weighed down by energy and gold stocks after the price of the precious weakened overnight.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12px;">Today&rsquo;s shortened trading session will now be followed by a New Years public holiday tomorrow ahead of trade resuming on Thursday.&nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Figures</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	The S&amp;P/ASX 200 index closed lost 5 points to finish the session at 5,352 &ndash; advancing from a starting point of 4,649 at the beginning of 2013.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The value of trades was $1.5 billion on volume of 317 million shares at the close of trade.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The top three stocks by value were BHP Billiton Limited (ASX:BHP), Commonwealth Bank of Australia (ASX:CBA) and Rio Tinto Limited (ASX:RIO).&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<br />
	On the futures market the SPI is 3 points higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>

	<strong>Economic news&nbsp;</strong></div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>

The RBA reports private sector credit grew at a steady rate of 0.3 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 3.8 per cent. Demand for housing credit rose 0.5 per cent in November for an annual growth rate of 5.1 per cent</div>

<div>
	The worst performing sector was energy, losing 48 points to close at 13,623 points.</div>
<div>
	<br />
	The best performing stock in the S&amp;PASX 200 was Forge Group Limited (ASX:FGE), rising 9.78 per cent to close at $1.74. Shares in Acrux Limited (ASX:ACR) and Slater &amp; Gordon Limited (ASX:SGH) also closed higher.</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The worst performing stock was Atlas Iron Limited (ASX:AGO), dropping 3.77 per cent to close at $1.15. Shares in Lynas Corporation Limited (ASX:LYC) and Horizon Oil Limited (ASX:HZN) also closed lower.&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	<strong>Commodities</strong></div>
<div>
	<br />
	Gold has posted one of its biggest annual losses in three decades. Snapping four days of upward momentum the price of the precious metal continued to pulled back today and is currently buying $US1,198 an ounce [Started 2013 at $US1,676 an ounce].</div>
<div>
	Light crude has slipped $1.03 today to $US99.29 a barrel [Started 2013 at $US98.82 a barrel]</div>
<div>
	<br />
	<strong>The Australian dollar&nbsp;</strong><br />
	&nbsp;</div>
<div>
	The Australian dollar is buying $US0.8923 [Started 2013 at $US1.039]</div>
